   vedatvaṃ vedatulyatvaṃ vā bhavatu; na śrutyādimūlakatve gauravāt,	veda-tvam veda-tulya-tvam vA Bavatu; na Sruti-Adi-mUlaka-tve gOravAt,
   nityabrahmayajñavidhiviṣayatvānupapatteśca, ṣaḍaṅgānāṃ tu "ṣaḍaṅgameke"	nitya-brahma-yajQa-viDi-vizaya-tva-anupapatteH-ca, zaxaFgAnAm tu "zaz-aFgam-eke"
   --- iti smṛterapi vedatvam /	-- iti smRteH-api veda-tvam /
   buddhabodhāyanamaśakādibhistu samākhyā	budDa-boDAyana-m-aSaka-AdiBiH-tu samAKyA
   kaṭhādivatpravacananimittatvenāpyupapanneti prāpte ---	kaWa-Adi-vat-pravacana-nimitta-tvena-api-upapannA-iti prApte ---
   dṛḍhakartṛsmaraṇātkaṭhādivatpravacananimittatvānupapatternaiṣāṃ vedatvaṃ	dRXa-kartR-smaraNAt-kaWa-Adi-vat-pravacana-nimitta-tva-anupapatteH-na-ezAm veda-tvam
   vedatulyatvaṃ vā /	veda-tulya-tvam vA /
   pratimanvantarañcaivaṃvidhānāṃ granthānāṃ	pratimanvantaraQcA-evaMviDAnAm granTAnAm
   sattvānnityabrahmayajñavidhiviṣayatvopapattiḥ /	sattvAt-nitya-brahma-yajQa-viDi-vizaya-tva-upapattiH /
   ekagrahaṇāttu "ṣaḍaṅgameke" iti paramatopanyāsaḥ /	eka-grahaNAt-tu "zaxaFgam-eke" iti parama-topanyAsaH /
   tasmādeṣāṃ smṛtyadhikaraṇanyāyena vedamūlakatvameva /	tasmAt-ezAm smRti-aDikaraNa-nyAyena veda-mUlaka-tvam-eva /
   śākyādigranthānāṃ tu tadasambhavāt ābhāsatvameva /	SAkya-Adi-granTAnAm tu tad-asamBavAt ABAsa-tvam-eva /
   <B2> (kalpasūtraprāmāṇyaparabhāṣyakārīyādhikaraṇaśarīrasya	<B2> (kalpa-sUtra-prAmANya-para-BAzya-kArIya-aDikaraNa-SarIrasya

   sā na yuktā; smṛtyadhikaraṇe vedātiriktavidyāsthānamātrasya vedamūlakatayā	sA na yuktA; smRti-aDikaraNe veda-atirikta-vidyA-sTAna-mAtrasya veda-mUlaka-tayA

   upalakṣaṇamabhipretya mlecchācārāṇāṃ keṣāñcidanāditvena śiṣṭācāratulyatayā	upalakzaNam-aBipretya mlecCa-AcArANAm kezAQcid-anAdi-tvena Sizwa-AcAra-tulya-tayA

   yuktamityanantarādhikaraṇavyutpāditaprāmāṇyopajīvanena	yuktam-iti-anantara-aDikaraNa-vyutpAdita-prAmANya-upajIvanena

   (kalpānāṃ sūtrāṇāṃ ca smṛtyadhikaraṇaviṣayatvena	(kalpAnAm sUtrANAm ca smRti-aDikaraNa-vizaya-tvena

   (prakāśakāranirūpitapūrvapakṣasiddhāntaprayojananirasanapūrvakasvābhimataprayojananirūpaṇam)	(prakASa-kAra-nirUpita-pUrva-pakza-sidDAnta-prayojana-nirasana-pUrvaka-sva-aBimata-prayojana-nirUpaNam)
   yattu --- prakāśakāraiḥ "vrīhīn prokṣati" "dadhnā juhotī" tyādau	yat-tu -- prakASa-kArEH "vrIhIn prokzati" "daDnA juhotI" tyAdO
   pūrvapakṣe sarvavrīhihomavyaktīnāṃ abhidhānāt tatra śrutyā	pUrva-pakze sarva-vrIhi-homa-vyaktInAm aBiDAnAt tatra SrutyA
   prokṣaṇadadhyāderviniyogāt prakaraṇasannidhibādhena laukikavrīhiṣvapi	prokzaNa-daDi-AdeH-viniyogAt prakaraNa-sanniDi-bADena lOkika-vrIhizu-api
   prokṣaṇaṃ homāntare ca dadhi syāt pūrvapakṣe, siddhānte tu	prokzaNam homa-antare ca daDi syAt pUrva-pakze, sidDAnte tu
   śabdārthabhūtāyā vrīhitvahomatvajāteḥ prākṛtavrīhihomayorapi	Sabda-arTa-BUtAyAH vrIhitva-homa-tu-a-jAteH prAkRta-vrIhi-homayoH-api
   paryāptisattvāt prakaraṇasannidhyanugrahe 'pi na kācicchrutipīḍeti	paryApti-sattvAt prakaraNa-sanniDi-anugrahe api na kAcid-Sruti-pIxA-iti
   prakṛteṣveveti /	prakRtezu-eva-iti /
   tat siddhānte 'pi prakṛtavrīhihomātiriktavyaktiṣvapi	tat sidDAnte api prakRta-vrIhi-homa-atirikta-vyaktizu-api
   tajjātiparyāptisattvenānivāraṇāt sarvaiśca	tad-jAti-paryApti-sattvena-anivAraNAt sarvEH-ca
   vyavahārāsaṃbhavenānarthakyaparihārārthaṃ prakaraṇādyālocanāvaśyakatvena	vyavahAra-asaMBavena-AnarTakya-parihAra-arTam prakaraNa-Adi-Alocana-AvaSyaka-tvena
   tena prakṛtātiriktānāṃ nivāraṇavat pūrvapakṣe 'pi tatsaṃbhavena	tena prakRta-atiriktAnAm nivAraNa-vat pUrva-pakze api tad-saMBavena
   viśeṣābhāvāt dvitīyādisthale lakṣaṇayā sarvavyaktibhānasyopapādanīyatvena	viSeza-aBAvAt dvitIya-Adi-sTale lakzaNayA sarva-vyakti-BAnasya-upapAdanIya-tvena
   doṣatādavasthyāccāyuktamityupekṣitaṃ pūjyapādaiḥ //	doza-tAdavasTyAt-ca-ayuktam-iti-upekzitam pUjya-pAdEH //
   iti navamamākṛtyadhikaraṇam //	iti navamama-AkRti-aDikaraNam //
   iti śrīkhaṇḍadevāntevāsikavimaṇḍanaśaṃbhubhaṭṭaviracitāyāṃ	iti SrIKaNxa-deva-antevAsika-vimaNxana-SaMBu-Bawwa-viracitAyAm
   bhāṭṭadīpikāprabhāvalyāṃ prathamasyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ //	BAwwa-dIpikA-praBAvalyAm praTamasya-aDyAyasya tRtIyaH pAdaH //
